                                local function v315()
                                    v288()
                                    if not _G.BaseSettings.showPreview then
                                        return 
                                    else
                                        local l_Center_0 = workspace.Map.Campground.MainFire.Center
                                        if l_Center_0 then
                                            v281 = Instance.new("Model")
                                            v281.Name = "StructurePreview"
                                            v281.Parent = workspace
                                            local l_Position_0 = l_Center_0.Position
                                            local v291 = l_Position_0.Y - l_Center_0.Size.Y / 2
                                            local l_radius_0 = _G.BaseSettings.radius
                                            local l_density_0 = _G.BaseSettings.density
                                            local l_floors_0 = _G.BaseSettings.floors
                                            local l_addDoor_0 = _G.BaseSettings.addDoor
                                            local v296 = math.rad(_G.BaseSettings.doorPosition)
                                            local l_doorWidth_0 = _G.BaseSettings.doorWidth
                                            local l_doorFloors_0 = _G.BaseSettings.doorFloors
                                            local l_addRoof_0 = _G.BaseSettings.addRoof
                                            local v300 = 2 * math.pi / l_density_0
                                            local v301 = l_doorWidth_0 / 100 * (2 * math.pi)
                                            for v302 = 1, l_density_0 do
                                                local v303 = (v302 - 1) * v300
                                                local v304 = false
                                                if l_addDoor_0 then
                                                    local v305 = math.abs(v303 - v296)
                                                    if math.pi < v305 then
                                                        v305 = 2 * math.pi - v305
                                                    end
                                                    if v305 <= v301 / 2 then
                                                        v304 = true
                                                    end
                                                end
                                                for v306 = 1, l_floors_0 do
                                                    if not v304 or l_doorFloors_0 < v306 then
                                                        local v307 = l_Position_0.X + l_radius_0 * math.cos(v303)
                                                        local v308 = l_Position_0.Z + l_radius_0 * math.sin(v303)
                                                        local v309 = v291 + (v306 - 1) * 39
                                                        local l_Part_0 = Instance.new("Part")
                                                        l_Part_0.Size = Vector3.new(2, 39, 2)
                                                        l_Part_0.Position = Vector3.new(v307, v309 + 19.5, v308)
                                                        l_Part_0.Anchored = true
                                                        l_Part_0.CanCollide = false
                                                        l_Part_0.Transparency = 0.5
                                                        l_Part_0.Color = Color3.fromRGB(100, 150, 255)
                                                        l_Part_0.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
                                                        l_Part_0.Parent = v281
                                                        table.insert(v280, l_Part_0)
                                                    end
                                                end
                                            end
                                            if l_addRoof_0 then
                                                local v311 = v291 + l_floors_0 * 39
                                                for v312 = -l_radius_0, l_radius_0, 2 do
                                                    for v313 = -l_radius_0, l_radius_0, 2 do
                                                        if math.sqrt(v312 ^ 2 + v313 ^ 2) <= l_radius_0 then
                                                            local l_Part_1 = Instance.new("Part")
                                                            l_Part_1.Size = Vector3.new(2, 39, 2)
                                                            l_Part_1.Position = Vector3.new(l_Position_0.X + v312, v311 + 19.5, l_Position_0.Z + v313)
                                                            l_Part_1.Anchored = true
                                                            l_Part_1.CanCollide = false
                                                            l_Part_1.Transparency = 0.5
                                                            l_Part_1.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 150, 100)
                                                            l_Part_1.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
                                                            l_Part_1.Parent = v281
                                                            table.insert(v280, l_Part_1)
                                                        end
                                                    end
                                                end
                                            end
                                            return 
                                        else
                                            return 
                                        end
                                    end
                                end

                                                local l_radius_1 = _G.BaseSettings.radius

                                                local l_doorFloors_1 = _G.BaseSettings.doorFloors
                                                local l_addRoof_1 = _G.BaseSettings.addRoof
                                                local v441 = 2 * math.pi / l_density_1
                                                local v442 = math.floor(l_density_1 * 0.5)
                                                local v443 = math.clamp(l_doorWidth_1, 1, v442) / l_density_1 * (2 * math.pi)
                                                local v444 = {}

                                                    local v446 = (v445 - 1) * v441
                                                    local v447 = false

                                                        end

                                                    local v453 = v432 + l_floors_1 * 39
